Emerald Nightmare Opens This Week
Normal and Heroic versions of Emerald Nightmare open this week! Mythic and Raid Finder Wing 1 open next week.

Check out our boss pages below for their abilities, loot, and encounter videos. Tier sets won't be coming until early 2017 when The Nighthold opens.

AskMrRobot - Free Premium Features for Monday and Tuesday
AskMrRobot (http://www.askmrrobot.com/) is making all of their premium features free through Tuesday (http://blog.askmrrobot.com/2016/09/get-ready-raids-free/)!

This includes the Best in Bags tool, which tells you which combination of gear that you currently have is the best. It also includes the Upgrade Finder tool that tells you what content still has upgrades for you.

Icy Veins - Emerald Nightmare Guides
Our friends over at Icy Veins are finishing up their Emerald Nightmare guides (http://www.icy-veins.com/wow/the-emerald-nightmare-raid), so be sure to take a look so that you are ready to go this week.

WoWProgress Profiles
WoWProgress (http://www.wowprogress.com/) has updated character profiles to show Artifact Traits (http://www.wowprogress.com/post/175_Artifact_details_in_character_profiles) and should be ready to go for the progression race!


http://media.mmo-champion.com/images/news/2016/september/wplaunchBanner.png (http://www.wowprogress.com/)


World Bosses
The world bosses will begin spawning this week! Killing them allows you to unlock another artifact appearance via Unleashed Monstrosities (http://www.wowdb.com/achievements/11160-unleashed-monstrosities). Several of them also dropped hidden Artifact appearances (http://www.mmo-champion.com/content/318-Legion-Artifact-Weapons-Info#hidden) in beta.


http://media.mmo-champion.com/images/news/2016/september/worldBosses.png (http://www.mmo-champion.com/content/595-Legion-World-Bosses)


Mythic+ Dungeons
Mythic+ dungeons open this week, with rewards that scale up along with the dungeon difficulty.

Dungeon

Every dungeon has a fairly forgiving timer you must beat to keep your keystone active.
You still get loot if you don't beat the timer, but your keystone becomes depleted.
As the keystone level increases, mobs in the dungeon do more damage and have more health.
The health and damage modifier is an almost linear increase, starting at 9% for Level 2 and increasing to 100% at Level 10.


Rewards

The max item level for rewards will be capped at 850 for the first week.
Rewards come from a chest at the end of the run, ranging from item level 845 at Mythic 2 to 865 at Mythic 10.
This chest contains two pieces of loot for the group, which is a change from beta.
You also get a weekly chest with loot based on your best run for the week, scaling from item level 860 to item level 880 at Mythic 10.
Rewards have a chance to be Warforged or Titanforged, allowing them to potentially scale all the way up to item level 895.
The only lockout on Mythic is the availability of keystones, you can keep doing them as long as someone has an active keystone.


Keystones

Check out Blizzard's official preview for Mythic Keystones (http://www.mmo-champion.com/content/5970-Class-Balance-Update-Honor-Talents-and-Prestige-Sept-14-Hotfixes-Mythic-Preview#mythic).
Keystones have modifiers that make the dungeon more challenging, with more being added as the keystone level increases.
New keystone modifiers appear at Levels 4, 7, and 10.
There is a list of keystone modifier pairs from beta (http://blue.mmo-champion.com/topic/407625-feedback-mythic-mythic-dungeons/#post3), but it may be outdated.
You can obtain a keystone by completing a Mythic dungeon or completing a Mythic+ dungeon run.
You also can obtain a keystone from your weekly chest, with a level slightly below your best run last week.
Each keystone only works for one Mythic+ dungeon and this is selected randomly upon creation or upgrade of the keystone.
Keystones will only select a dungeon that is unlocked for everyone in the group when it is modified.
Keystones are upgraded when you complete a Mythic+ dungeon, with the amount of the upgrade determined by how much you beat the timer by.
If you don't beat the timer, your keystone will be depleted.
Depleted keystones can still be used to start additional runs, but those runs won't give a loot chest at the end.
If you do beat the timer on a depleted keystone run, your keystone will be upgraded and empowered again, so you can attempt the next difficulty level for loot.

Keystone Master</a> <span class="subtext">Participated in the realm-first completion of a Level 15 or higher Mythic dungeon within the time limit.</span> </td></tr></tbody></table></td><td class="c"></td><td class="c">Feats of Strength</td></tr> </tbody></table>


Overflowing - Healing in excess of a target's maximum health is instead converted to a heal absorption effect.
Skittish - Enemies pay far less attention to threat generated by tanks.
Volcanic - While in combat, enemies periodically cause gouts of flame to erupt beneath the feet of distant players.
Necrotic - All enemies' melee attacks apply a stacking blight that inflicts damage over time and reduces healing received.
Teeming - Additional non-boss enemies are present throughout the dungeon.
Raging - Non-boss enemies enrage at 30% health remaining, dealing 100% increased damage until defeated.
Bolstering - When any non-boss enemy dies, its death cry empowers nearby allies, increasing their maximum health and damage by 20%.
Sanguine - When slain, non-boss enemies leave behind a lingering pool of ichor that heals their allies and damages players.
Tyrannical - Boss enemies have 40% more health and inflict up to 20% increased damage.
Fortified - Non-boss enemies have 20% more health and inflict up to 40% increased damage.



Legion PvP Season 1
The first Legion PvP season starts on Tuesday!


Legion PvP seasons will be shorter than they have been in the past.
The Gladiator gear uses Tier 19 models (http://www.mmo-champion.com/content/1407-Tier-19-Armor-Sets).
Mark of Honor (http://www.wowdb.com/items/137642-mark-of-honor) will be available from rated PvP.
Two new arenas were added: Black Rook Hold and Ashamane's Fall.
Season one will reward the Vindictive Gladiator's Storm Dragon (http://www.wowdb.com/items/141843-vindictive-gladiators-storm-dragon)

ejpaints
2016-09-22, 05:05 PM
They could break the ingame zygor addon.

Why should they? Zygor charges $5 a month for access to all of their guides for multiple games including non blizzard ones. They offer an addon for the games that have addon support, but the fee isn't specifically for that addon, it's for access to all of the guides on the site. I've used it on multiple games, the fee covers all of them. The addon does the exact same thing that conslegion addon does, only better bc it's been around longer. But, my $3 a month (since I purchased the guide quite a long time ago I get a discount), goes towards access to more than just the wow leveling guide. Literally the only difference between the ones with an addon support & the ones without is that it's a whole lot nicer when I don't have to be tabbed out to figure out what side quest I'm missing for a loremaster achieve is.

I get some people don't like the guides, I do. It helps me not miss things. It helped me go back & finish loremaster title during MoP since I had no idea where I'd stopped in Darkshore for example, & it was especially helpful in directing me to all of the things in Suramar that were easily missed if I didn't go to that area. I'm a completionist. So breaking the addon wouldn't stop me from using their guide, it would just annoy me that I had to keep it open on my other monitor to use it.
